name:H‚Äçs‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço
info:Superior Queen Room
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted April 8, 2023
msg:Pullman hotel is always a great choice when staying in Yantai.  It's got a great location next to the Wanda Plaza which has good shopping and restaurants, as well as across the street from this very ancient style looking area which also has good shopping, restaurants, and some bars.  Rooms are very clean and our view of the ocean was great.  The staff is very polite and helpful from when i checked in to when I checked out, only person's name I remember was Alice Sun. There is also a really cool robot that can bring your food deliveries up to your room if you ask.  

The only recommendation I would have is it would be really great if there was a more direct pathway to the Wanda Plaza.  Currently, you have to walk out the front of hotel and walk around the entire corner to get to the Wanda Plaza.  Not a big deal at all but it would be great if there was a pathway or steps from when you exit the hotel, go directly to your left into the parking lot and can walk right down to the Wanda Financial Center over to the Wanda Plaza.  Saves you an extra few minutes. :)
